 rigerv bank ne kaha ki 100 rupee ke karency note main suraksha visheshtaayen badhaai gai hai
 Under this, the numbers in the number panel will be increasing in size
 rigerv bank ne mahatma gandhisiris- 2005 main 100 rupeke bank note jari kiya he jismensankhya praturupanaya he
 The central bank said that now the numbers in both the number panels of these banknotes will be increasing in size from left to right
 isamen shuru ke teen akshar or ank (alphanumeric) aakaar main ek samaan honge
 According to the Reserve Bank, giving numbers in increasing order is a security feature so that common people can easily differentiate between correct and fake notes
